\hypertarget{deca__regs_8h_a0ddac39358a872ee845cf042c7ef8976}{\#define \hyperlink{deca__regs_8h_a0ddac39358a872ee845cf042c7ef8976}{R\-X\-\_\-\-T\-T\-C\-K\-I\-\_\-\-I\-D}~0x13            /$\ast$ Receiver Time Tracking Interval (in double buffer set) $\ast$/}\label{deca__regs_8h_a0ddac39358a872ee845cf042c7ef8976}

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Bit definitions for register R\-X\-\_\-\-T\-T\-C\-K\-I The value here is the interval over which the timing offset reported in the R\-X\-T\-O\-F\-S field of Register file\-: 0x14  R\-X\-\_\-\-T\-T\-C\-K\-O is measured. The clock offset is calculated by dividing R\-X\-T\-T\-C\-K\-I by R\-X\-T\-O\-F\-S. The value in R\-X\-T\-T\-C\-K\-I will take just one of two values depending on the P\-R\-F\-: 0x01\-F00000 @ 16 M\-Hz P\-R\-F, and 0x01\-F\-C0000 @ 64 M\-Hz P\-R\-F. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\subsection{Detailed Description}
D\-W1000 Register Definitions This file supports assembler and C development for D\-W1000 enabled devices.

\end{DoxyAttention}
